first disease resistance trait for Sclerotinia resistance.<br><br>Begins commercialization process for its three developed traits with initial transfers to customers&#58; pod shatter reduction in canola and HT1 and HT3 in rice.<br><br>Opens first stand-alone high-throughput (gene editing) breeding facility for trait production to support the commercial launch of its first three developed traits across canola, winter oilseed rape, and rice, and the development of its advanced traits.<br><br>The European Union proposes new regulation for new genomic techniques (NGTs) that would regulate Cibus&#8217; traits such as pod shatter reduction and Sclerotinia disease resistance as &#34;conventional-like&#34; (breeding).<br><br>Signs collaboration agreement with Bayer Ag to evaluate Cibus&#8217; Trait Machine&#8482; platform and capabilities.<br><br>Management to host a conference call webcast Thursday, August 10th at 8&#58;00 a.m. ET</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">  </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">SAN DIEGO, August 9, 2023 &#8211; Cibus, Inc. (Nasdaq&#58; CBUS), </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">a leading agricultural technology company that develops and licenses plant traits to seed companies</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">, today announced its financial results for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2023, and provided a business update.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8220;Since January, when Cibus Global, LLC and Calyxt, Inc. signed an agreement to merge, the combined company has made incredible progress hitting our established milestones, including closing the merger transactions on May 31, 2023, and, in so doing, beginning to establish Cibus&#8217;&#160;high-throughput plant breeding&#160;platform as a standard for plant based gene editing,&#8221; stated Rory Riggs, Chairman and CEO of Cibus, Inc. &#8220;This year we began commercializing our first three trait products by sending customers initial transfers of their elite germplasm with Cibus traits. We also made significant progress in the advancement of the next three traits in our pipeline.&#34; Mr. Riggs continued, &#34;In addition, we opened the world&#8217;s first&#160;stand-alone high-throughput trait development facility for editing plants to support the commercial expansion of our trait business. Finally, and most importantly, we are seeing customer demand for our offerings, evidenced by the signing of multiple breeding collaborations with major global seed companies.&#8221;<br><br>As part of our breeding collaboration programs, Cibus is pleased to share that it has recently </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:12pt;text-align:center"><img alt="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" src="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" style="height:72px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:294px"></div></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">entered into a collaboration agreement with Bayer Ag to evaluate Cibus&#8217; Trait Machine, its </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">high-throughput (gene editing) breeding</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> platform, and capabilities. Cibus will leverage its Trait Machine process anchored by its patented Rapid Trait Development System&#8482;, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">RTDS&#174;,</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> to evaluate new techniques applicable to Bayer Ag germplasm. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Stated Mr.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> </font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Riggs, &#8220;Cibus&#8217; </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">RTDS</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:107%"> </font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">is the set of proprietary technologies used in the Trait Machine process to integrate crop specific cell biology platforms with a series of gene editing technologies to enable a system of end-to-end crop specific precision breeding. Importantly, the traits from the Trait Machine are indistinguishable from traits developed using conventional breeding or from nature. Under the European Commission's July 2023 proposed regulations, products from Cibus&#8217; </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">RTDS</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> gene edited traits would be regulated as &#8220;conventional-like&#8221; (breeding) traits, as they already are in the United States. Cibus believes that </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">RTDS</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> and the Trait Machine process represents a technological breakthrough in plant breeding that is the ultimate promise of plant gene editing&#58; high-throughput gene editing systems operating as an extension of breeding programs.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8220;The merger and the achievements of our 2023 milestones are important elements of our business plan. Together they provide critical building blocks in establishing Cibus in the trait business and in our position as a leader in high-throughput (gene editing) plant breeding. Our recent collaboration agreements, such as today&#8217;s announcement of our breeding collaboration with Bayer Ag, move us closer to establishing our vision of high-throughput plant breeding operating as a technological extension of conventional breeding programs.&#8221; Added Mr. Riggs. &#8220;In our vision, the goal is to establish crop-by-crop collaborations with seed companies to develop a new era of plant traits that can make farming more productive and profitable and address the sustainability needs in each crop created by climate change.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Major Milestones Achieved in 2023</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:14pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%"><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">First transfers of Cibus' three developed traits to customers in their elite germplasm. The first trait transfer was Cibus&#8217; pod shatter reduction trait in canola, which was transferred to Nuseed in its elite germplasm. Following that transfer, in April 2023, Cibus transferred its HT1 and HT3 traits in rice to Nutrien in its elite germplasm.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">The opening of Cibus' 32,000 square foot Oberlin facility in San Diego which houses its proprietary Trait Machine&#8482; process. This is the first semi-automated, high-throughput, end-to-end, trait production system providing a time bound, predictable, and reproducible breeding system for gene editing of commercial plants. The facility provides Cibus with the gene editing production capacity to support the commercial launch of its first three developed traits across canola, winter oilseed rape, and rice. This facility will also be central to Cibus' expected soybean trait business.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">In addition to its three developed traits, Cibus has three additional traits in development. Two of these traits, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> resistance and HT2, are progressing through the greenhouse and to the field. </font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Cibus announced that additional greenhouse test results had demonstrated successful resistance against white mold, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia,</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> in canola. These greenhouse tests showed both an enhanced and an additional mode of action from previously noted field trial results of the Cibus </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia </font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">resistance trait. Together, these two different modes of action provide an increased level of resistance against </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> than each alone. The </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia </font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">resistance trait is expected to enable yield improvement, cost reduction, and lower usage of fungicides.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:12pt;text-align:center"><img alt="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" src="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" style="height:72px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:294px"></div></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">In July 2023, as part of its Farm to Fork initiative, the European Union proposed new regulations for New Genomic Techniques (NGTs). Under the proposed regulations, if adopted, Cibus&#8217; traits such as pod shatter reduction and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> disease resistance, would be regulated as &#8220;conventional-like&#8221; (breeding). If approved by the EU Parliament and Council (Member States), this change would be a watershed moment for the trait business. It would open up the gene edited trait business to the 100 million plus acres of farmland in the EU. In addition, it would be a critical point of inflection for the progress globally to treat gene edited traits like conventional breeding.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Future 2023 Milestones</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">In addition to the milestones that Cibus has already accomplished this year, Cibus has several important milestones that it expects to accomplish in the second half of 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Successfully validate its Trait Machine process in a customer&#8217;s elite soybean germplasm. In addition, Cibus expects to begin editing in its soybean platform in 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Transfer up to five additional seed company partners its pod shatter reduction trait in the customers&#8217; elite germplasm.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Initiate field trials in the UK for winter oilseed rape.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Release additional greenhouse and field data associated with its </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Sclerotinia</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> resistance trait and its HT2 trait.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Initiate editing for its initial mode of action for nitrogen-use efficiency in canola.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Enter into additional breeding collaborations in North America and South America for its HT1 and HT3 traits.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Second Quarter 2023 Financial Results</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font as of June&#160;30, 2023, was $50.9 million. The Company believes cash and cash equivalents will enable Cibus to fund planned operating expenses and capital expenditure requirements</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"> into the first quarter of 2024</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Research and development (R&#38;D) Expense&#58;&#160;R&#38;D expense was $8.4 million for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2023, compared to $3.2 million in the year-ago period. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">The increase of </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">$5.2 million is primarily related to increased lab supply and facility expenses, an increase in employee headcount, and an increase in stock-based compensation expense for restricted stock award grants and the acceleration of share vesting associated with stock award agreements due to the acquisition of Cibus Global, LLC. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%"><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font expense&#58; SG&#38;A expense was $11.1 million for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2023, compared to $3.6 million in the year-ago period. The </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">increase </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">of $7.5 million is primarily related to an increase in headcount, increased consulting and legal fees, and an increase in stock-based compensation expense for restricted stock award grants and the acceleration of share vesting associated with stock </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:12pt;text-align:center"><img alt="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" src="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" style="height:72px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:294px"></div></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">award agreements due to the acquisition of Cibus Global, LLC.<br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Non-operating income (expenses)&#58; Non-operating income was $1.3 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2023, compared to $4.3 million in the year-ago period. The decrease of $3.0 million in non-operating income is due to changes in the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">fair </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">value of the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">liability classified </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Class A common stock warrants. <br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Net loss&#58;&#160;Net loss was $20.5 million for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2023, compared to $2.5 million in the year-ago period.<br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt;padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%;padding-left:12.03pt">Net loss per share of Class A common stock was $(3.05) for the quarter ended June&#160;30, 2023, compared to $(2.66) in the year-ago period.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Conference Call and Webcast Information&#58;</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#160;Cibus will host a live webcast on Thursday, August 10, 2023, at 8&#58;00 a.m. Eastern Standard Time&#160;to discuss its second quarter 2023 financial results and provide a business update. To access the live webcast, go to </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">the investor relations section of Cibus&#8217; website at https&#58;&#47;&#47;investor.cibus.com&#47;news-events&#47;events. Interested parties participating by phone will need to register using this form&#58; https&#58;&#47;&#47;register.vevent.com&#47;register&#47;BI6b5a9b78bcd44a15a38e13475fa10226. After registering for dial-in details, all phone participants will receive an auto-generated e-mail containing a link to the dial-in number along with a personal PIN number to use to access the event by phone. Following the event, a replay will be archived there for 30 days under the investor relations section of Cibus&#8217; website at https&#58;&#47;&#47;investor.cibus.com&#47;news-events&#47;events.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">About the Trait Machine Process (the Trait Machine&#8482;)</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">The Trait Machine is a dedicated semi-automated end-to-end process for precision gene editing that delivers trait products that integrate into our seed company customers' breeding programs. It is a process of gene editing at scale and speed that uses the world&#8217;s best crop genetics (a seed company&#8217;s elite germplasm or seeds). The Trait Machine is based on Cibus&#8217; proprietary Rapid Trait Development System&#8482;, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">RTDS&#174;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">. Under the recent European Commission's proposal on regulation of plants obtained from new genomic techniques, such as the traits from the Trait Machine would be regulated as &#8220;conventional-like&#8221; (breeding).<br><br>Cibus believes that RTDS and the Trait Machine represents a technological breakthrough in plant breeding that is the ultimate promise of plant gene editing, a dedicated &#8220;industrial&#8221; breeding process at scale whose trait products are indistinguishable from conventional breeding or nature, and a process that provides the ability to change the scale and range of possible genetic solutions from breeding and with it, to develop the desired characteristics or traits needed for greater farming sustainability and food security with greater speed and accuracy.<br><br>Cibus&#8217; recently opened the Oberlin Facility which is the first dedicated Trait Machine facility. It is modeled on high quality biologics manufacturing processes from the pharmaceutical industry. The Trait Machine process is crop specific. It is currently operational for canola, winter oilseed rape, and rice. Cibus plans to extend this to soybean, corn, and wheat. Cibus expects the soybean platform Trait Machine process to be operational in the second half of 2023. The promise is that, at scale and with the additional Trait Machine crop platforms, Cibus will be able to launch important multi-crop traits simultaneously across multiple crops.</font><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%"><br><br></font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-top:12pt;text-align:center"><img alt="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" src="cibus_logoxrgba.jpg" style="height:72px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:294px"></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#fefefe;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:125%">About Cibus</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Cibus is part of the multi-billion-dollar plant seed industry. Cibus is the leader in the new era&#160;of high-throughput gene editing technology that can develop plant traits&#160;precisely and predictably at a fraction of the time and cost of conventional breeding. Cibus is not a seed company. It is a technology company that develops and licenses traits to seed companies in exchange for royalties on seed sales. Cibus&#8217; target market is productivity traits that improve yields, lower input costs such as chemicals, and increase the sustainability and profitability of farming. It has a pipeline of six productivity traits including important traits for pod shatter reduction, disease resistance, and nitrogen-use efficiency. Cibus&#8217; focus is scale, multi-crop traits that can impact greater than 100 MM acres.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.05pt;margin-top:0.05pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Forward Looking Statements</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:0.08pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">This press release contains &#8220;forward-looking statements&#8221; within the meaning of applicable securities laws, including The Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
